 9 percent

 Yes, what you wear at bedtime also makes a big difference in your sleep
 shodhakartaaon ke mutabik, coton (sooti) yaa poliester kaa pyjama pahanane ke bajaae oonee kapade pahanane se gahari neend lene main madad mil sakati he
 Dr
 of The University of Sydney paul swen ne bataaya, kuch samay pehle woollen bed par sone kaa chalan tha or ab vigyaan oonee kapade pahanakar sone ke phaaydon kii phir se khoj kar rahaa he
 He said, 'this is no coincidence
 woollen aapke sharir ke taapmaana ko zyada behatar dhang se niyamit karte hai jise thermal comfort jone bhi kaha jaataa he
 'research suggests that people who wear woolen pajamas, especially when the cold rises at night, they sleep early
 isse naa keval ve zyada der tak neend le pate hai balki acchhee or gahari neend lene main bhi madad milti he
 It has become very difficult to get good sleep in today's busy life
 aise main agar kisi bhi cheez se madad milti he to ye aapaki mental or physical health ke liye acha he
 The researchers conducted two studies
 pehali study main 17 bacchon ko shaamil kiya gaya jinhone coton yaa merino wool ke pajame pahane
 While the second group consisted of 36 adults between 50–70 and were given to wear polyester, cotton
 donon studies main heart rate, skin temparechar, relative humidity or brain wave ke pattern ko mapa gaya
 The group of young adults with woolen clothes slept 7 minutes more than those who wore cotton
 in logon ko 15 minute ke bheetar hi neend aa gai, vahiin coton vaale samooh ko 15 minute lage
 At the same time, Woolen outperformed cotton and polyester in the group of older people
 65-70 saal ke logon ko oonee kapadon main 12 minute main neend ai jabaki poliester or coton main 22, 27 minute lag gaye
 The author concluded that this suggests that wool is a good insulator and can affect skin warming
 kul milakar yah acchhee or gahari neend ko badhaava detaa he
 This study has been published in the journal Nature and Science of Sleep

 bydaree ke sahare gafoor mohammad kaa dil dhadkane laga
 32-year-old Mohammed came to India from Kurdistan with his wife Dilkara

 tippaniyan The timings of buses and trains were constantly being announced from loudspeakers in the fair area, so that the passengers could get the correct information and not to go to the bus or railway station before their scheduled time
